Home Mobiles Phone Finder Nokia 207. SPECIFICATIONS USER REVIEWS NEWS. Share on Facebook Tweet Share Share Email Reddit. Nokia 207 mobile was launched in July 2013. The phone comes with a 2.40-inch display with a resolution of 240 pixels by 320 pixels. It comes with 64MB of RAM. The phone packs 256MB of internal storage that can be expanded up to 32GB via a microSD card. As far as the cameras are concerned, the Nokia 207 packs a No primary camera on the rear The Nokia 207 is powered by a 1020mAh removable battery. It measures 114.20 x 50.90 x 12.80 (height x width x thickness) and weigh 91.30 grams. The Nokia 207 is a single SIM (GSM) mobile that accepts a Micro-SIM. Connectivity options include Bluetooth, Headphones, FM and 3G.. Nokia 207, Nokia 208, Nokia 208 dual-SIM feature phones unveiled. More Nokia mobiles Nokia mobiles price in India. No Autofocus Without Autofocus, the camera of the mobile is will not be able to focus on the subject automatically. Light Weight - 91g Lightweight mobile phones are easier to carry and look more fashionable. You cannot store more songs, photos and videos. Low Battery Life - 1020 mAh Lower Battery Life causes quick battery drain & results in frequent charging. Nokia 207, Nokia 208, Nokia 208 dual-SIM feature phones unveiled. Surbhi Chawla , 03 July 2013. Share on Facebook Tweet Share Share Email Reddit Comment. Nokia has unveiled three new feature phones, which will start retailing from the third quarter of 2013. These handsets are dubbed Nokia 207, Nokia 208 and Nokia 208 dual-SIM. These smartphones will be available for $68 (before local taxes and operator subsidies) and will support 3.5G HSPA. 2.4-inch QVGA display 256 MB RAM Expandable storage up to 32GB Bluetooth 3.0, 3.5G HSPA 1020mAh battery 114.2 x 50.9 x 12.8mm 89.63 grams 2.4-inch QVGA display 1.3-megapixel rear camera 256 MB RAM Expandable storage up to 32GB Bluetooth 3.0, 3.5G HSPA 1020mAh battery 114.2 x 50.9 x 12.8mm 90.59 grams. The Nokia 207 , Nokia 208 and Nokia 208 dual-SIM are candy-bar phones that come with Nokia Xpress Browser, which as per the company claims helps in compressing data by up to 90 percent.. In addition to this, popular social networking apps such as Twitter, Facebook and WhatsApp will come pre-installed on these mobile phones. Users can also download apps from the Nokia Store. One of the interesting applications that is available the new phones is the Transfer app. With the help of this app, users can easily import contact details from other phones, including Windows Phone 8 and most of Android smartphones.. Mail for Exchange functionality is fully supported on the Nokia 207, Nokia 208 and Nokia 208 dual-SIM. The phones also comes with Bluetooth 3.0 with Slam sharing , that lets people share stuff over Bluetooth without the need of pairing phones first.. The Nokia 207, Nokia 208 and Nokia 208 dual-SIM come with 2.4-inch QVGA display and support expandable storage via microSD card up to 32GB. These phones come with a 1020mAh battery, which as per the company's claims gives 12 hours of talk time on a 2G network for the single SIM variant, and standby time of more than a month. The Nokia 208 and Nokia 208 dual-SIM come with 1.3-megapixel rear camera.. It's worth noting that Nokia 207, Nokia 208 and Nokia 208 dual-SIM use a micro SIM and not a standard SIM. All the three smartphones will be available in Red, Cyan, White and Black colour options.. Nokia 208/ Nokia 208 dual-SIM key specifications. Nokia is a Finnish mobile phone manufacturer that was dominant in the 1990s and early 2000s. The company was unable to compete with the likes of Apple and Samsung when touchscreen smartphones gained popularity, thus rapidly losing market share. Nokia's mobile unit was acquired by Microsoft, which renamed the company as Microsoft Mobile.. The new Nokia 207 is a basic feature phone featuring a 2.4-inch QVGA LCD display with a screen resolution of 240x320 pixels. It is powered with a 256MB RAM and has the same internal memory of 256MB that is expandable up to 32GB via microSD card. On the connectivity front the device includes 3G, Bluetooth, GPS and EDGE as its features. Nokia 207 is fuelled by 1020 mAh battery which provides decent battery backup providing up to 490 hours of standby time and 12 hours talk time in 2G network and upto 500 hours of standby time and 4.5 hours talk time in 3G network as well as maximum music playback time of 29 hours. The device lacks a camera but comes preloaded with applications like Facebook, Twitter and Nimbuzz. The Nokia 207 is a basic phone that offers 2.4'' display, 64 MB RAM, 256 MB user memory, Bluetooth 3.0 and Facebook and Twitter built-in. Dimensions: 4.50 x 2.00 x 0.50 inches (114.2 x 50.9 x 12.8 mm). Weight: 3.22 oz (91 g) the average is 5.6 oz (159 g). Features: Numeric keypad, Soft keys, D-Pad. Colors: Black, Yellow, Blue, Red, White. Resolution: 240 x 320 pixels. Pixel density - The pixel density of a display represents the number of pixels over an area of one inch. It’s measured in “pixels per inch”, or ppi. The higher the number, the more detailed and good-looking the display is.. Technology - There are two main screen technologies currently used in phones and tablets: LCD and AMOLED. The former usually features a light source and liquid crystals, while the latter is based on organic light-emitting diodes. Newer LCD variations like IPS-LCD and Super-LCD allow for very accurate color reproduction and very wide viewing angles, where no significant image quality loss is observed. Current AMOLED screens differ in such a way that they can exhibit much more saturated colors (sometimes too much) and incredibly high contrast levels, which is due to black color being completely black in AMOLED displays.. Screen-to-body ratio - Shows what part of the frontal area of a phone its screen occupies.. 0.06 GB RAM / 256 MB ROM. System memory - System memory, or RAM memory is the type of memory that the device uses to temporarily store data from the OS or currently-running apps. The more RAM available to the device, the better the performance will be when multiple or heavier programs are running.. Storage expansion - Some handsets allow you to expand their storage capacity by using a memory expansion card – most often microSD. Expansion memory is mostly suitable for media storage, such as photo, video or music content.. Talk time: 12.00 hours the average is 20 h (1229 min). Stand-by time: 20.4 days (490 hours) the average is 21 days (502 h). Talk time (3G): 4.50 hours the average is 19 h (1147 min). Stand-by time (3G): 20.8 days (500 hours) the average is 25 days (590 h). Capacity - The bigger, the better! However, battery capacity is not the only factor that has an effect on battery life. Those include the chipset in use, the software running on the device, as well as the consumer's unique usage pattern.. Cellular GSM: 850, 900, 1800, 1900 MHz. Data: HSDPA 7.2 Mbit/s, HSUPA 5.76 Mbit/s. Phone features Notifications: Music ringtones (MP3), Polyphonic ringtones (32 voices), Vibration, Speakerphone. Features: Mass storage device, USB charging. Positioning - This field shows the positioning systems supported by the device. The most common types are GPS and A-GPS.. GPS - This is one of the most widespread global positioning technologies, developed and maintained by the U.S. It uses satellites in order to detect your location. A-GPS - A-GPS stands for Assisted GPS and is the industry standard for positioning and navigation. “Assisted” means that it can use local wireless networks, in addition to satellites, for quicker and more precise localization.. Availability Officially announced: 03 Jul 2013. FCC approval - The Federal Communications Commission (FCC) is an independent United States government agency, directly responsible to Congress. The FCC was established by the Communications Act of 1934 and is charged with regulating interstate and international communications by radio, television, wire, satellite and cable. The FCC's jurisdiction covers the 50 states, the District of Columbia, and U.S. Every wireless phone device that is sold in the U.S. has to be tested and approved for sale by the FCC.. Date approved - Shows the date when the particular phone is approved by the Federal Communications Commission. FCC ID value - Shows the FCC Identifying value of the particular phone. FCC measured SAR - Working closely with federal health and safety agencies, such as the Food and Drug Administration (FDA), the FCC has adopted limits for safe exposure to radiofrequency (RF) energy. These limits are given in terms of a unit referred to as the Specific Absorption Rate (SAR), which is a measure of the amount of radio frequency energy absorbed by the body when using a mobile phone. The FCC requires cell phone manufacturers to ensure that their phones comply with these objective limits for safe exposure. Any cell phone at or below these SAR levels (that is, any phone legally sold in the U.S.) is a "safe" phone, as measured by these standards. The FCC limit for public exposure from cellular telephones is an SAR level of 1.6 watts per kilogram (1.6 W/kg).. To see the full specifications with in-depth details click here.. When you purchase a cell phone it is often offered at a discounted price by the cellular network. In return for this generosity they "lock" your Nokia 207 Unlock Code to their network, so that you can only use their network for making and receiving calls. This means that you cannot use the SIM card of another network, and if you try to do so the phone will display "Phone Restricted", “Contact Service Provider”, “Enter Unlock Code” or a similar message. Unlocking the phone removes this lock, allowing you to use your Nokia 207 Unlock Code on any GSM wireless network anywhere in the world. A SIM card or Subscriber Identity Module is a portable memory chip used in GSM phones. The SIM Card allows users to change phones by simply removing the SIM Card from one cell phone and inserting it into another. The SIM holds personal identity information, cell phone number, phone book, text messages and other data. How does the remote unlocking work?. Upon successful order submission, we will process your Nokia 207 Unlock Code's unique IMEI number and email back an unlock code. The International Mobile Equipment Identity or IMEI is a 15 digit serial number unique to every GSM cell phone. We generate the unlocking code from the IMEI, this is called remote unlocking. Enter *#06# into your phone to retrieve the unique 15 digit IMEI number. It can also be found printed on the back of the phone underneath the battery. No software or cable is required at all.
